On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 83.8 degrees and the lowest was 69.1 degrees.

Correspondence 162

To the Esteemed Editors of the Shenbao Newspaper:

With utmost respect, we, the tea workers formerly hired by the Minxing Anji Steamer Company's "Hu Da" steamship last July, sought employment and, following the company's regulations, paid deposit fees. Now that the company has suspended its voyages, we have repeatedly negotiated for the return of our deposits, but to no avail. We are all poor villagers and farmers who rely on our labor for a living. The sudden loss of a large sum of money has left us without employment, forcing us to wander the streets of Shanghai for months. We have pawned everything and can no longer borrow money, leaving us hungry, cold, and in extreme distress. As a last resort, we petition the Party and government authorities to order the company to return our deposits and to request appropriate compensation for our losses, so that we may return to our hometowns. At the same time, we appeal for sympathy and assistance from all sectors of society. We have long admired your newspaper's commitment to justice and your support for the oppressed, which prevents the poor and weak from suffering innocently. We have temporarily set up an office in Yangjiadu Houjie, No. 16, Nanshi, to notify the affected tea workers to register and negotiate. We earnestly request that your esteemed newspaper publish this in the news column so that the truth may be known and we may receive assistance to achieve our goal. We would be immensely grateful. With sincere respect, we await your favorable response.

Respectfully submitted by the Petitioning Group of Tea Workers of the Minxing Anji Steamer Company's "Hu Da" Steamship, Shanghai.

To the Editors of the Shenbao Newspaper:

Having read your newspaper's news column on June 2nd, which stated that the market price of animal intestines continued to rise, we find it to be inconsistent with the facts. Our member, Guo Shunji, does not have branch factories in northern Anhui or southern Henan. Even considering the stock in Shanghai, there is a significant accumulation. The market price of raw materials began to fall in May. The claim that there is a market but no goods is purely fabricated. We cannot guarantee that someone is not deliberately spreading rumors to disrupt the intestinal industry market. We request that this be corrected.

Respectfully submitted by the Shanghai Special City Pig Intestine Trade Association, June 6th, Year 19.

To the Editors of the Shenbao Newspaper:

Our client, Mr. Zhang Tianji, informs us that he has read your newspaper's report on June 3rd, titled "Repercussions of Zhang Tianji's Accusation Against Zheng Fuyu." The report mentioned that yesterday, oppressed clerks from the Changlu Salt Smuggling Prevention Bureau submitted a letter to your newspaper. We are unaware of the identities of these so-called oppressed clerks. Can they provide names and take responsibility for their claims? If there are such people who have truly been oppressed, Tianji has been out of office for a year. Why have they not formally reported it until now? The content of the letter is merely a cunning attempt by the defendants Zheng Fuyu and Lu Hongshi (also known as Huanquan) to justify themselves in the case of intimidation and fraud. It is obvious at first glance. We do not hesitate to clarify further as follows:

The letter stated that Tianji embezzled over 1,400 yuan in private case rewards and refused to distribute them, despite repeated requests from the clerks. However, all rewards received by Tianji during his tenure at the Changlu Salt Smuggling Prevention Bureau were distributed monthly. Zheng Fuyu, in particular, received rewards and borrowed hundreds of yuan in advance. He continues to harass us repeatedly. At that time, there were more than a dozen clerks in the bureau, and no one ever mentioned the distribution of rewards, let alone the so-called repeated requests from the clerks. Although a petition signed by Xie Zhen has been submitted requesting the distribution of rewards, a truthful reply has been filed. However, when Zheng was arrested, the detectives from the Huishi Police Station found a directive from Xie Zhen Nong on Zheng's person, indicating that the so-called "claimants" are still under Zheng's influence.

Furthermore, Zheng and Lu Hongshi fabricated allegations that Tianji engaged in illegal embezzlement and dereliction of duty, without any evidence. They claimed to have printed 5,000 copies (as stated in their letter) and distributed them to various Party and government agencies in an attempt to blackmail him. When Tianji reported the arrest of Zheng, the so-called evidence was found on him, including a list of Tianji's appointed personnel. This list should have been handed over to the successor for record-keeping, but Zheng stole it during the handover to use as blackmail today. His premeditation is clear. Another piece of evidence was an order from Tianji detailing the investigation of any commissioned personnel who were absent from their posts. This was a document for Tianji's rectification of his department. How can it be considered evidence of illegal embezzlement? A third piece of evidence was a letter from Tianji's wife, Zhang Sun Xiuzhen, to Li Qishan. This letter was written out of compassion to request a contribution for the family of a deceased employee, Zhu Guoxiang. How can it be construed as a loss to the government? The rest of the allegations, such as "setting traps" and "preemptive strikes," are merely attempts by Zheng and others to clear their names and are not worth discussing.

We have been entrusted to convey the above information and request that you publish this letter in your esteemed newspaper as a rebuttal.

Respectfully addressed to the Editors of the Shenbao Newspaper,

Lawyer Wang Siji, June 5th.

To the Editors of the Shenbao Newspaper:

Having seen the report in today's newspaper regarding the Xin Da Kiln Factory workers assaulting the police corps, we have learned that there are some inaccuracies.

(1) When the police corps came to search the workers, it was still before dawn, and Pei Cang was not notified. Pei Cang only tried to mediate when someone reported that the workers were arguing about the matter and refusing to work, but it had already become a stalemate.

(2) There are a total of seven workshops, all located outside the factory, about half a mile away. Therefore, the police corps searched the workshops, not the factory itself.

(3) The workers did not resist during the search. It took about two hours to search all seven workshops completely. Afterwards, since no stolen goods were found, the workers questioned Deputy Corps Commander Gong. Instead of comforting them, Gong used harsh official language, which angered them and led to the assault.

(4) Gong and Wang are currently receiving medical treatment at Shanghai Hospital. They sustained minor injuries and will be discharged soon.

The above are all facts and should not be dismissed summarily. We have already submitted a request to the county government to send personnel for a thorough investigation to ensure a fair resolution to this case. We would be grateful if your esteemed newspaper could publish this letter.

Respectfully submitted by He Pei Cang, owner of the Xin Da Kiln Factory, June 6th.

Educational News - Sports

The Chinese Team Returned Safely to Shanghai Yesterday Morning 164

Welcome Home, Athletes! ... Friends and Relatives Extend Greetings

From Now On, Put in the Effort ... Vow to Wash Away the Shame of This Session

More than a hundred Chinese athletes from the 9th Far Eastern Games, led by General Representative Zhang Boling, Hao Boyang, and others, returned triumphantly aboard the Ryuta Maru yesterday. Ma Xunbo, the representative of the Ministry of Education, Zhao Jinqing and Lin Kanghou, representatives of the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education, and Xu Minhui also returned with the ship. Dr. Wang Zhengting's representative, Chen Shiguang, Zhou Jiaqi and Yu Hengzhi of the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education, Zhao Tiezhang, and over a hundred athletes, relatives, and friends came to the port to welcome them. The Bund pier became a bustling scene. The welcome flags of the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education stood high above the crowds, like a demonstration of the masses' welcome. The ship was spotted as the bell rang nine times. The sound of firecrackers rose, and the cheers overflowed the air. The ship docked at half-past nine. Our country's athletes, who had been separated for two weeks, were reunited with their hometown, shaking hands and exchanging warm greetings. The scene of the send-off was still fresh in their minds, but each person's psychology had undergone a different transformation. The reporter gathered a wealth of information and will provide a brief account after returning and preparing.

Two Representatives Speak 165

Zhang Boling, the General Representative of the Chinese team, told reporters that the Chinese team's failure this time was not due to a lack of progress in their performance, but rather because their progress was not as rapid as that of others. He also said that he has already devised methods to address both the symptoms and the root causes of our country's physical education (detailed in an interview with this newspaper's reporter in Japan). The day of gradual implementation, collaboration, and hard work is not far off. Zhao Jinqing, the representative of the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education and the Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, told reporters that it is undeniable that the Chinese athletes' performance was not as good as others. However, their spirit and character demonstrated the attitude of a great nation, which was praised by people from other countries. He also said that after visiting various industrial factories, he had a profound impression: the Japanese are too eager for progress, while the Chinese are too slow to improve. Both extremes are not beneficial.

Secretary Xu's Great Contribution 166

Xu Zhendong, the Deputy Secretary-General, handled all the miscellaneous affairs of the Chinese delegation in Japan appropriately and in an orderly manner. Many praised his diligent service and considered him one of the most hardworking and contributing members of the entire delegation.

Three Earthquakes Encountered 167

The athletes encountered three earthquakes in Tokyo: the first on the 23rd, the second on the 28th, and the third on the 30th. The first two earthquakes were not major, but as strangers in a foreign land, they could not help but turn pale at the mere mention of it. The third earthquake occurred suddenly late at night, and many people were caught off guard and rushed out of their rooms without dressing properly, creating a chaotic and amusing scene.

The grand scene of the Chinese team's arrival at the port yesterday morning (Photo by Tian Xiang)

Qiu and Lin Compared 168

Qiu Feihai and Lin Baohua, the Chinese tennis representatives, gave different impressions during the various competitions in this session. Qiu gave his best effort in every match, regardless of winning or losing. The Japanese regarded him as a formidable opponent. Lin enjoyed showing off and winning but could not accept defeat. The Japanese considered him a showman rather than a competitor. However, Lin is young and strong. If he can change his ways and strive for progress, his future is limitless.

Filipinos' Misconduct 169

The athletes from the four countries lived together in one place. The Chinese and Japanese athletes were well-regarded for their proper conduct due to strict management. The Indian athletes were also quite self-disciplined. However, some of the Filipino athletes often engaged in undisciplined behavior due to lax restrictions. Their secret relationships with Japanese women drew criticism from the Japanese.

Japanese Progress 170

The Japanese dominated the tournament, displaying courage everywhere. Even in the football and basketball events, where they had previously lagged behind, they showed obvious improvement. In football, they had mastered the art of passing and cooperation. Their only weakness compared to the Chinese was in the final shot at the goal. In basketball, they adopted a man-to-man defense strategy, resulting in much better results than before. The Japanese spirit of fierce pursuit is admirable.

The Stain on the Tournament 171

The Japanese organized this tournament magnificently, with grandeur beyond description. However, their excessive ambition led them to abandon fairness and means in pursuit of immediate victory. The referees' one-sided bias was met with dissatisfaction from both China and the Philippines and was a stain on the tournament.

Returning Home 172

Of the more than one hundred athletes returning to Shanghai, a portion of the Tianjin athletes will be led back to Tianjin by Zhang Boling in the coming days. The South China football, men's and women's volleyball, and swimming athletes will also return to their hometowns.

Sun Guiyun Arrives in Harbin 173

Harbin, June 6th (This newspaper's dispatch) - Five athletes from the Special District, including Sun Guiyun, who attended the Far Eastern Games, returned to Harbin on the 6th.

Methods to Promote Chinese Sports 174

Emphasis on physical education in schools of all sizes, national guidance by experts.

Football teams sent to Europe for practice, volleyball and basketball teams divided into North and South to train.

Zhang Boling's Remarks on the Return Journey (Special Correspondent Qian Hua of this Newspaper)

Mr. Zhang Boling, the General Representative of the Chinese delegation, is known for his enthusiasm for sports. During several long conversations with Zhang on the ship back to Shanghai, the reporter discussed in detail the methods to promote Chinese sports in the future. It is only with the awakening and efforts of the people of the entire nation and the promotion of the government that the future of Chinese sports can be optimistic. Not only will there be no hope of victory four years from now, but China will eventually have no place at the Far Eastern Games. This failure is enough to make us wake up and seek remedies urgently. It is still not too late. Mr. Zhang said:

Japanese Progress is Formidable 175

After going to Japan this time, I have many feelings. The progress of the Japanese in everything is admirable and formidable. Sports is just one aspect. Track and field and swimming are already comparable to those of countries around the world. Even in football and basketball, the strength three years ago was like heaven and earth. This spirit of unremitting struggle is truly worthy of our emulation.

Photograph of General Representative Zhang Boling after Returning to Shanghai (Photo by Sun Daosheng)

Referee Issues in the Future In this tournament, the lack of experience of the referees and their bias were unpleasant. Regarding this point, our country's representatives raised it at the Three-Country Representatives Meeting and requested that each country pay attention to it. As a result of the discussion, it was decided that when the next tournament is held, the referees should first seek the consent of the other two countries, but because this article concerned Japan's reputation, it was not recorded in the minutes of the meeting but was limited to the understanding of the three countries.

Fundamental Remedies Zhang also said that regarding the fundamental remedies for the decline of Chinese sports, the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education held a meeting on the Ryuta Maru on the morning of the 5th to discuss and decide on two methods: treating the symptoms and treating the root causes. The fundamental remedy is to formally suggest to the Ministry of Education to increase the compulsory physical education courses from elementary school to university, and then to have appropriate instructors responsible for guiding, classifying, and gradually engaging in practice. However, this cannot be achieved in the short term.

North-South Regional Training As for the symptomatic treatment measures decided on that day: (1) Football will focus on the Hong Kong and Shanghai teams for training, and in the short term, funds will be allocated to send them to Europe for competition to increase their experience. (2) Volleyball will be the responsibility of the Hong Kong and Guangdong teams to continue practicing, hiring excellent coaches to strive for progress with the latest scientific methods. (3) Basketball will focus on Tianjin and Beiping for training, and regional competitions will be held from time to time, with the proceeds from the sale of tickets used to cover the travel expenses of the two teams. (4) Track and field competitions will be promoted throughout the country. Training will be conducted in various schools. Efforts will be made to build more sports fields. Swimming and baseball are the most immature and difficult sports in our country. Building a state-of-the-art 50-meter swimming pool is extremely costly, but the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education should still try to find ways to make progress. For the time being, various sports practices will be aimed at the National Games next year, so that we can be more motivated.

Reorganizing the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education Someone suggested reorganizing the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education to form a strong physical education center. I also deeply feel that the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education is incomplete. The Association for the Advancement of Physical Education was originally divided into five regions: Southeast, Central, Northwest, with North China having a longer history and more unity. But I firmly believe that the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education must have a central force that can control the whole country, and Shanghai is the most suitable location. Without the Shanghai organization, the seventh session would not have been able to go to Manila to participate in the conference, the eighth session would not have been able to be held in Shanghai, and this session would not have been able to be held. Moreover, before the Chinese sports undertakings were hosted by foreigners, since the seventh session, they have been completely autonomous by the Chinese. It must not be said that there is no progress. Everything must progress gradually, and overexertion is prone to obstruction, so I advocate that we should temporarily maintain the status quo and take the opportunity to convene national physical educators during the National Games next year to discuss a complete reorganization. There are also those who advocate that the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education should also take provinces and cities as units, and I am afraid that it will be more difficult to convene the whole country, which is not a good plan.

Nankai School Sports Mr. Zhang said that he was deeply moved by this visit. After returning to Tianjin, he should take Nankai School as a model and start physical education training, making physical education a compulsory course from elementary school to university.

Hire good coaches to train in various fields and plan to build large and medium-sized basketball rooms, each taking next year's National Games as its goal, maintaining the name of the Tianjin basketball team, and taking a step further to increase the strength of the national basketball team by one point.

Diary of the Chinese Athletes' Return Journey 176

(Qian Hua)

Enjoying the Scenery of Nikko and Yokohama, the Joy is Harmonious

The Separation of North and South Athletes at Ueno, Reluctantly

After the Far Eastern Games closed on May 31, the Philippine delegation took a night train to Osaka at 9:30 p.m. to participate in the International Games on June 1 and 2. Since our country's results were too far behind, it was decided in advance not to participate, so there was a tour of Nikko on June 1.

(1) Visiting Ryugu in Nikko 177

At 6 a.m. on June 1, the entire Chinese delegation of hundreds of people set off from the Japan Youth Center and went straight to Ueno Station. After taking a train from Ueno to Nikko, they arrived in Nikko at about 10 a.m. Nikko is one of the ten famous scenic spots in Japan. The mountains are green and the water is clear, and the scenery is extraordinary. After getting off the train, they took a short rest and had breakfast at the nearby Ryugu Hotel. Then, they went out to tour separately. Sun Sijing and other football players stayed at Ryugu because their legs were injured and they were not able to walk well. They said that they were happy to visit Ryugu in Nikko, which was a self-deprecating joke.

(2) Viewing the Living Horse and Visiting the Dragon Statue 178

Near the Ryugu Hotel, there is a temple with a rough scale. The courtyard has a very large horse stable with a brown and white horse, which is majestic and tall, showing extraordinary quality. The leader said that this horse was ridden by Emperor Taisho before his death. After Taisho's collapse, this horse was left here to be taken care of in old age to show its excellence. There is also a room in the inner courtyard of the temple with a dragon statue hanging inside. It is said that if you clap your palms at the statue, you can hear the dragon's roar, but the room is limited to one person. Our crowd did not get a practical experience. I think it is a type of Chinese magic.

(3) Shaking Hands, Heartbroken Tears 179

After leaving the temple, male and female athletes dispersed to various places. Most of the small stalls made exquisite small wooden boxes. The opening and closing mechanisms were quite popular with the female athletes. They bought them one after another, and none of them were less than three times more profitable. The second was the wind photo, which was kept as a souvenir. At 4:25 p.m., the entire delegation finished the tour and took a car back to Tokyo. They arrived at Ueno Station at 7 p.m., and the North and South athletes also parted ways in Ueno. The athletes from Harbin, Liaoning, Beiping, and Tianjin took a car to Busan and went to Liaoning and Shanghai via Korea, while the Guangdong athletes took a car to Yokohama and stayed on the Ryuta Maru. The North and South athletes had been together for several months, and they were close like brothers and sisters. Once they were separated, they were all sad. The emotions of the female athletes were particularly rich, and some even cried out loud. Sun Guiyun and Huang Shuwei were especially sad. In the end, Huang Shufang cried. The station was full of sorrow. The whistle called out again and again, and I don't know when we will meet again in the north and south. Truly, there is no feast in the world that does not end.

(4) Consul Held a Tea Party 180

The delegation of Shanghai and Guangdong athletes, led by Zhang Boling, Hao Boyang, and others, took a car from Ueno to Yokohama at 9 p.m. After arriving at the port, the local overseas Chinese came to the station to welcome them and invited them to a Cantonese restaurant for dinner. They were treated with courtesy and sincere enthusiasm. After the meal, the whole group stayed on the Ryuta Maru. The next morning at 9 a.m., the Consul General in Kobe held a tea party in the consulate to entertain them, and there were various entertainment activities that doubled the fun. At 10:30 a.m., they returned to the wheel and set sail for Kobe at 11 a.m.

(5) Situ Guang Won a Silver Cup 181

On the morning of the 3rd at 8 a.m., the ship arrived at the local overseas Chinese Zheng Boling and his wife, as well as three representatives of the Kobe Prefectural High School Women's Volleyball Team (former representatives of the Japanese Women's Volleyball Team) boarded the ship to welcome them. Zheng handed over the donations to Hao and presented the volleyball championship team with a large silver cup in the name of the Osaka and Kobe Overseas Chinese Support Association, and also presented a silver cup to Situ Guang for winning a valuable point for the country in this competition as a souvenir. That evening at 7:30 p.m., Zheng Guoheng, the comprador of the Kobe Horan Small Public Bank, hosted a banquet. Mo Yinggui, the deputy coach of the delegation, accompanied him. The guests included He Shichang, chairman of the Kobe General Chamber of Commerce, Huang Shudian, a merchant, and Lin Zifan, the manager of the Tianjin Zhongyuan Company. At the same time, Zheng's sons, Boling and his brothers, invited Xu Zhendong, football player Li Huitang, volleyball captain Cao Tingzan, and tennis stars Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai. Cao Yanhua, Ren Fubo, and other gentlemen attended the meeting. They talked about the sports industry for a long time until 10:30 p.m., when the guests and hosts dispersed in joy. On the morning of June 4, the Kobe Prefectural First High School Women's Volleyball Team hosted a welcome party for our country's women's volleyball team. At 12 noon, they set sail for Shanghai.

Zhao Jinqing, Representative of the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education (Photo by Tian Xiang)

(6) Peaceful and Happy Wind and Waves 182

Since sailing at noon on June 4, the wind and waves have been calm all the way. Male and female athletes have been walking on the deck and playing various games. Xu Zhendong, Lin Shihua, Qiu Feihai, and Smith personally paid for the upgrade from third class to second class. The athletes complained that the food in third class was too bad, so they negotiated with the ship to change to eating second class food.

Among the staff, Zhang Boling, directors Zhao Jinqing, Lin Kanghou, and others were sitting in second class. The food intake of our country's athletes is very large. After changing to second-class food, they were able to fill their stomachs.

(7) Opening a Meeting to Decide on a Strategy 183

At 10 a.m. on the morning of June 5, the entire Chinese delegation was gathered in the passenger room to hold a meeting. General Representative Zhang Boling was the chairman. Zhao Jinqing, Lin Kanghou, and Ma Xun, who was sent by the Ministry of Education to observe the Far Eastern Games, were also present. First, Mr. Zhang Boling gave a speech, saying that the tournament showed the extraordinary progress and special efforts of the Japanese everywhere, but the lack of experience in refereeing was a shortcoming. Our country's failure this time was a good lesson. We should work together and strive to the end. Next, Zhao Jinqing gave a speech, saying that the most gratifying thing about this tournament was that the spirit of our great country was brought into full play. The most obvious things were (1) the discipline was solemn, and there were no facts such as the Philippines making various jokes, etc. (2) Although the referees on the other side were extremely unfair, our athletes were able to endure it to the end and never left the field halfway. Next, Lin Kanghou gave a speech, saying that if China wants the true development of sports, the education authorities must formulate regulations and implement compulsory physical education in primary and secondary schools. Next, Ma Xun gave a speech, proposing three points: (1) Please the Ministry of Education to implement compulsory physical education. (2) Find ways to train specialized coaches. (3) Promote the chivalrous spirit of sports. Then, Mo Yingji, the representative of the Hong Kong team, proposed to reorganize the Association for the Advancement of Physical Education. After detailed discussion, it was considered that the status quo should be maintained temporarily, and the reorganization should be implemented after the National Games next year. Next, they discussed the remedies for Chinese sports, so as to restore a considerable position in four years, and decided to carry out two methods of treating the symptoms and treating the root causes (the methods decided are detailed in another article, Zhang Boling's speech). Finally, head coach John Ma gave a speech, saying that although our country returned in failure this time, judging from the results of track and field, the athletes exceeded all domestic results, indicating that there was progress, but not as fast as others. We should not be disappointed and should work harder to make progress and hope to say less empty words and focus on practicality. The crowd applauded greatly, and the meeting adjourned at 12 noon.

(8) Yearning to Return Home 184

That night, the advertisement on the ship read that it would arrive at the Waibaidu Bridge Wharf at 9 a.m. tomorrow (the 6th). The Shanghai athletes were all delighted, especially Mr. Lin Baohua, who said that he could meet his mother tomorrow. He was very proud. At 7 a.m. on the 6th, it had already entered the Wusongkou. Male and female athletes were all leaning on the railings and looking into the distance. Before long, it was near the Waibaidu Bridge Wharf. The welcome flags and firecrackers could be seen and heard. The athletes' joy was indescribable. The so-called yearning to return home is like an arrow, and the reporter's diary also came to an end.

Lin Baohua vs. Sato 186

Sato started the serve and won two sets in a row. Since the third set, Mr. Lin had a very good performance. In the third and fourth sets, Sato repeatedly lost points due to serving and smashing. Until Mr. Lin took the lead with a score of 4-2, Sato saw a turning point and won four sets in a row in one go, making a score of 6-4 and winning the first game.

At the beginning of the second game, Sato still had the upper hand. Mr. Lin won two balls first in the first set and lost four points in a row. In the second set, Mr. Lin only got one ball. In the third set, Sato had a very strong and accurate push ball. In the fourth set, Mr. Lin won two balls. In the fifth set, Mr. Lin was completely defeated. In the sixth set, Mr. Lin won one ball. He lost with a score of 6-0. In the last two sets, Mr. Lin was very difficult to support. He let Sato hit and could not fight back.

In the third game, Mr. Lin struggled to his strength. In the first two sets, he had a great momentum to recover the game. Sato only got one ball each. Qiu Feihai versus Bu Jing 187

After Bu Jing served the opening ball, both sides each won a set. Bu then won three sets in a row, making the score four to one. At this point, Qiu used extremely accurate and low, long shots to counter the opponent, which proved to be quite effective. He won five points in six sets, taking the lead with six to five. In the following two sets, he lost due to carelessness. However, Qiu, with his rich experience, was able to rally even though he was at a disadvantage with a score of seven to six. He won two sets. In the end, Qiu showed some fatigue and was unable to run as much, ultimately losing to Bu Jing with a score of eight to ten.

In the second game, after Bu served the opening ball, he won a set. Afterwards, each side won two, making it two to two. However, Bu advanced bravely and scored three points in a row. Qiu also did not show weakness and won the eighth set. Finally, Bu won another set with an angled shot, thus winning the game with a score of six to three.

At the beginning of the third game, Qiu's response became more fierce, eager to recover the lost ground. His long shots were quite effective, but he was already exhausted. Therefore, even though he ran as hard as he could, he often failed to return the opponent's ball. He lost the first set after two tie balls. The second set also became a tie ball. Just as he was trying hard to resist the incoming ball, he suddenly collapsed due to leg cramps and showed a very painful condition. After medical treatment, he was still unable to move, so he declared his withdrawal in order to rest and then play doubles tomorrow.

Qiu's performance was excellent. His shots were very steady, accurate, and fast, making it impossible for the enemy to

predict. It is a pity that his physical strength was slightly weak and he could not withstand a long battle, which led to his defeat. It is truly a pity.

forward to follow

Labor University Actively Proceeding 198

The National Labor University is the only highest institution of labor education in the country. It has been established for three years. It is said that the university department was originally divided into two colleges, Industry and Agriculture. Later, with the approval of the Ministry of Education to add a College of Social Sciences, the name of the College of Social Sciences of the university had a problem due to the promulgation of the University Organization Law. The Ministry of Education recently issued an order to temporarily suspend enrollment. However, the university's enrollment brochure has already been printed and issued, making it difficult to suspend. The university's President Yi is currently negotiating with the Ministry of Education to temporarily allow enrollment. New Buildings of Daxia University Will Be Completed 199

Daxia University purchased more than 150 mu of school land next to Sun Yat-sen Road in Fan Huangdu last year to build permanent school buildings because the original Jiaozhou Road school buildings were not enough. The first phase of construction started on January 5 of this year, including a large classroom building, a steel-concrete structure, 200 feet long and 80 feet wide, with three floors. There are more than 30 classrooms, laboratories, and reading rooms, which can accommodate more than 2,000 people in class at the same time. There are two male dormitories, each 200 feet long and 150 feet wide, each with three floors, which can accommodate a total of more than 1,400 students. There is one female dormitory, 200 feet long and 100 feet wide, with three floors, which can accommodate 400 students. The large classroom has been built to the third floor, and each dormitory has been built to the second floor. They will all be completed in early August, and all of them can be moved in by the end of August. The summer school and summer enrollment matters of the school are still held in the Jiaozhou Road school buildings. The new school of the school is all

The equipment is the most up-to-date. The classrooms are equipped with automatic electric bells, and an electric clock is installed at the highest point of the large classroom. There is no need to ring the bell or blow the horn for class. The desks are all newly made iron frames with Liu'an wood surfaces. Each person in the dormitory has an iron bed and a Liu'an wood self-study desk. Each two people share an electric lamp. In terms of water use, there is a self-drilled artesian well that can draw 170,000 gallons of water per day. A water tower is built to filter the drinking water and divert it to various places for use. All the equipment and utensils of the school have been carefully planned, and manufacturers have been invited to sign contracts for the undertaking, all of which will be completed in early August. All the utensils in the current Jiaozhou Road school buildings will be left for the middle school department to use and will not be removed because the middle school department will move to the Jiaozhou Road school buildings next semester. The new school site of the school faces Sun Yat-sen Road and is close to Zhaofeng Park. The No. 3 and No. 7 bus stops are all on Sun Yat-sen Road, very close. It is also heard that after moving in, the school will have several public buses to travel back and forth directly to the center of Shanghai, which is even more convenient.

Laugh It Off Hai Ke 202

A: My old wife and I have been married for thirty years and we are always polite. There has never been a disagreement, and there has never been a sound of quarrels.

B: Poor man, your life is so monotonous, aren't you bored to death?

Beggar: Sir, please have some mercy. I have a wife and four children at home who all depend on me for food.

Miser: We are truly in the same boat. I have two wives and eight children at home who all depend on me for food.

Eye Patient: Sir, I have suffered a lot for these eyes.

Doctor: Then why did you come for treatment? Isn't it much easier without eyes?

Old Gentleman: Child, you are sixteen years old this year, why are you still short like you haven't grown up?

Child: I study too hard, I am busy all day long and I don't have time to grow up.

Father: If you don't cut off ties with that prostitute, I will cancel the allowance I give you every month.

Son: If you don't double my allowance, then I will marry her.

Contrary Fish 203

Ji Qin

The contrary fish is a special product of my lake. It is about four or five inches long, shaped like a river perch with round lips and a broad back. The belly is solid and has roe. It is taken and dry-fried with oil and a little spice. It does not spoil overnight and can be sent by mail. As I live overseas, my relatives and friends often send it to me as a taste of home. Why do I need to feel the pain of only enjoying perch in the autumn wind?

The fish is named contrary, and many people do not understand it. I have heard the elders say that this fish is also called Xun fish. The best ones are produced in Xunxi Creek of the lake. Every year in April and May, when the yellow plum rain rises and the creek flows rapidly, they do not measure their own strength and lead their companions to go against the current. Fishermen catch them with nets, filling thousands and hundreds, and if one escapes, it will eventually be cooked for people to eat. The book says that those who obey heaven will survive, and those who go against heaven will perish. This is why this fish is contrary. I specifically record it for verification.

Yi Baisha's Drowning in the Sea by Bing 204

Everyone knows that the old lunar calendar Dragon Boat Festival is the day when Qu Yuan drowned in the river. Dragon boats and zongzi are offered by the river to mourn. To this day, this custom has not declined in Jingchu. But who knows that in Qu Yuan's hometown, ten years ago today, someone also drowned in the sea on the Dragon Boat Festival? I will write a record of Yi Baisha's drowning in the sea.

Yi Baisha, named Kun, styled Yuecun, was from Changsha. He lived in Baisha Well and admired Chen Wengong of Baisha, so he called himself Baisha. When he was young, he read Zheng Suonan's History of the Mind and the books of the Ming Dynasty hermits, and he suddenly felt the pain of the race. When he heard the revolutionary anti-Manchu theory of the Min Party, he was overjoyed and befriended the Min Party members. During the Xinhai Wuchang Uprising, Anhui responded, and Sun Yujun was the governor. Baisha was in Anhui and organized students with Han Qibai and others to form a youth military. The Yuan-suppressing campaign was dissolved, and he fled to Japan and published the Jia Yin magazine with Zhang Xingyan and others. Yuan's was defeated and returned to the country to teach. He wrote articles for the New Youth magazine several times and also contributed to the Construction magazine. His works such as Kongzi Pingyi and Emperor's Spring and Autumn were all published in this period. Later, Sun Yat-sen presided over Guangzhou and advocated the Northern Expedition. Baisha went to visit him and stated his willingness to form a team to accompany him to conquer the bandits. Hu Zhantang and Zhang Puquan said that you should serve the country with articles, not go to danger. Baisha took a small steamboat to Chencun on the night of the Dragon Boat Festival, left a paper with a white hat on the seat, and jumped into the sea. Chencun is the hometown of Chen Wengong of Baisha. When the incident was heard, the authorities were shocked. The sea was searched for ten days, but the body could not be found. A pavilion and a monument were built to commemorate him.

Baisha devoted himself to the study of the various schools of thought and history, advocating Mo and rejecting Kong, and his actions were close to chivalry. As for the Emperor's Spring and Autumn, he listed all the chief culprits and great evils who had harmed the people for thousands of years in our country. He said in the preface that I read four thousand years of history and saw that those who harmed the people most deeply and for the longest time were none other than the holy ancestors and benevolent ancestors, while the harm of Jie, Zhou, You, and Li was quick and obvious, far better than benevolent government. Therefore, Zhang Taiyan's Baisha Zi Fu said that in ancient times, there were those who lived in turbulent times and were angry and made rambling words, or those who were not Tang Wu and did not despise Zhou Kong and were left behind, such as Zhuang Zhou and Yinruo Ji Kang. Their words were like turbulent rapids, all inwardly forgiving themselves and outwardly measuring the world, and they were not self-consciously. Baisha Zi is close to them.

Baisha drowned in the sea on the fifth day of the fifth month of the Republic of China at the age of thirty-six. His brother Peiji printed his Emperor's Spring and Autumn to be published.

What I Saw in Singapore 205

Xu Shiqi

Singapore is located in the south of the Malay Peninsula, commanding the Strait of Malacca, the throat of Euro-Asian transportation, and it is the tripod with Saigon, French Indochina, and Colombo, British Ceylon. During my trip to Europe, I took a boat to the port and got a tour. The mountains are green and the sea is clear, and the chest is refreshed by the high outlook. Then, Hu Wenhu and Qiu Jiyao, the consuls general of the Tang Dynasty in Singapore, and the reporters from various newspapers boarded the boat to welcome them. The public gathered on the deck and scrambled to take pictures. Mr. Minyi introduced them to me one by one, and then followed Mr. Lin Fachu's appointment for breakfast at his residence. The Malay cuisine is full of exotic flavors, which are rarely seen in China. My wife, Manhua, found it difficult to chew because the taste was different. After the meal, several kinds of fresh fruits were served. In addition to mangoes, oranges, and bananas, there was also Luguoguo (translated) , a Malay specialty that is shaped like a walnut, has the texture of lychee, and tastes particularly good. The host earnestly persuaded me to eat a lot. During the banquet, Mr. Lin and Mr. Chu talked about the past and expressed their feelings, and sighed that the old comrades were fading away, which led to a sense of vicissitudes. Mr. Lin is an advanced figure in the Party-State, a famous industrialist, and has deep ties with Mr. Jingjiang Zhantang and Jingwei. He has made great contributions to the revolution of the Premier. In 1905, he organized the Tongmenghui in Singapore and used Wanqingyuan as the site of the conference. This was the beginning of the Tongmenghui, which has a very glorious and great history for the National Revolution. Mr. Lin has a rich collection of Premier's manuscripts, which is enough to cherish. In the future, he will publish it and let the world see it. Then Mr. Chen Jiageng came to visit, looking extremely humble, with a clear and thin face, and he seemed unable to speak. Because I did not know the Min dialect, I could not talk to him. After sitting for a while, I left and asked me to visit the factory at a certain time.

At about 10 o'clock, I drove to Johor for a visit. Johor is a small country in the Malay Peninsula, like Luxembourg in Europe. In 1885, it signed a treaty with Britain and became a protectorate. The people are lazy and their nature is decadent. I walked along Bukit Timah Road for 17 miles to reach the Strait of Johor. A causeway of one mile was built. This causeway was completed in 1927, took five years, and cost 30 million gold. The stones of the two mountains were dug to build it. There is a section of iron bridge at the entrance, with machines for lifting and lowering to allow boats and cars to pass. A military port is built next to it to fortify the sea defense. The great project of the Straits Settlements is the greatest of these. Passing through the Johor palace, the structure of the palace is not as magnificent as imagined. Mr. Qiu Jiyao told me that when Mr. Hu Zhantang came here a few years ago, he once built a real palace, and the contents and equipment were like a museum. He ascended the throne and became a temporary foreign king, so he clapped his hands and laughed. Today, the King of Johor is favored by the British and accompanies his queen (the British gave her a concubine's room to act as a concubine). He travels west to Jilv and is unable to return. After visiting his imperial garden, the green grass is like a carpet, the trees are lush, and the lonely palace wall is worth remembering. We drove back quickly, and it was already past noon, so we followed the appointment of the Tang Consul to have a dinner at the Chinese Club. Mr. Tang is the son of Mr. Shaochuan, and he has been in Singapore for a year, and his political reputation is outstanding. At 2 o'clock, we visited the Chen Jiageng Company factory, which is located at the intersection of North Bridge Road and Samba Wa Road in Singapore. The area is vast, covering more than 10 acres. Mr. Chen Jiageng kindly received us and explained in detail. The factory has a total of 5,000 workers, of which female workers account for two-thirds. The fund is about 10 million or more. The largest product is rubber shoes, which can produce an average of 25,000 pairs per day. In addition to selling to various provinces in the country, it has now expanded its foreign trade and opened a branch in the UK to promote it. If it manufactures tarpaulins, rubber wheels, rubber tires, canned food, printing, soap, felt hats, etc., it is colorful. It took one or two hours to see the whole picture, which shows the vast scope of the company.

Record of the Characteristics of Russian Literature and its Women 206

By Xiaochang

My close friend, Mr. Li Zihua, has lived in Russia for many years. This time, upon his return to China, he described the nature of the Russian people in great detail. Now, I record one or two of these descriptions to introduce them to my fellow countrymen.

The characteristic of Russian literature is its genuineness and frankness. This is especially evident when comparing Russian novels with English ones. English novelists express their own opinions and release their pent-up spirits. Although adorned with beautiful prose, the true essence of the author's soul is not fully revealed. Russians, however, are different. They are unrestrained and genuine, not only pouring out the author's true feelings and vividly portraying them, but also presenting the truth of society and its characters with honesty. From this, one can understand their energy and mood, see their nature and sincerity. The strengths and weaknesses can also be discerned. A single reading of a novel by a famous Russian author reveals the true face of farmers, criminals, and madmen. There are those who plot social reforms, those who oppose them, those who view them with indifference, those who admire the Orient, those who are enthusiastic about the West, and those who respect their own country. Although diverse and chaotic, all are presented with truth. The nature of Russian literature is indeed similar to that of English women's literature.

Another characteristic of Russian novels lies in their depiction of human emotions. No matter how excellent a work may be, if it does not portray human emotions, it will not be valued by society. What Russians admire is human emotion. It can be cruel, it can be vulgar, it can be fierce, it can be pitiful, but it is best when it can express human emotions. Therefore, Russian novelists value human emotions over law, religion, morality, and the hearts of sages. They meticulously depict the feelings of adulterous women and the states of mind of madmen, striving to capture the truth.

Russian women can be found in all aspects, not just in literature. When emotions arise strongly, they truly desire to put them into practice. If they cannot put them into practice, they transform into melancholy. This is the common trait of women and also the common trait of Russians. According to reports, many great Russian scientists are women, many great literary figures are women, and even in politics, religion, and party movements, there are many women. It can be said that the nature of the Russian people is indeed close to that of women.

A Grand Gathering of Relatives at the National Revolutionary Army Orphans' School 207

By Wang Shangyi

The National Revolutionary Army Orphans' School, located outside Zhongshan Gate in the capital city of Nanjing, held its third relatives' meeting on the afternoon of May 31st. As one of the family members, I was fortunate enough to participate in this grand event. Therefore, I will record the proceedings of the meeting with my pen.

History and Content of the School: After establishing the capital, the central government, deeply concerned with the achievements of the martyrs, specifically established this school in the winter of the seventeenth year to educate and nurture their orphans. The purpose is noble and sufficient to comfort the heroic souls. A preparatory committee was established to manage and construct the school, overseeing its completion. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Cai Yuanpei, and eight others served as committee members. Madam Soong Ching-ling is the principal. Initially, the school was located in Dacang Garden in the city. The school buildings were insufficient, so land was purchased near Sifangcheng to build more than twenty school buildings, which can accommodate two to four hundred students. Currently, there are primary and secondary school departments and a vocational department. The monthly expenses are allocated by the Ministry of Finance. All student clothing, food, and supplies are provided by the school. The school has facilities such as a hospital and a library. The dormitories and cleaning rooms are very well-maintained. In terms of teaching, emphasis is placed on practicality. Therefore, the secondary school department has vocational and agricultural courses, continuing through winter and summer. Students can continue their studies. In addition to reading, students are responsible for all daily work in the school. This is the characteristic of the school. The school is located in a quiet area with excellent air quality. Therefore, studying here is not only academically beneficial but also beneficial to the body. In the future, serving the country and society will surely bring comfort to the martyrs in the afterlife.

Grand Opening Ceremony: At one o'clock in the afternoon, relatives, guarantors, teachers, staff, and students of the entire school, totaling over five hundred people, attended the meeting. First, Ms. Zhang Shengyi, the director of school affairs, and the teachers led the guests to visit the school buildings and the achievement exhibitions. There were over a thousand pieces of exhibited achievements, a dazzling array of achievements rarely seen in primary and secondary schools. The silkworm cocoons and various specimens from the agricultural science department were particularly excellent. After the visit, the meeting began. Director Zhang delivered a school affairs report, followed by student performances. There were ten items, including Butterfly and Remembering Jinling, mostly dances. The sound of the piano never ceased. Next was the performance of The God of Peace, depicting the tragic story of the May Thirtieth Movement. It greatly enhanced patriotic spirit. The performances by the primary school students, full of childlike innocence, were especially endearing. After the performances, there were speeches by family members, followed by refreshments and photographs before the event concluded.

Eastern Travel Correspondence (6) 208

By Wu Xiaohou

(Chou) A Brief Overview of Tokyo City Administration: The Tokyo Municipal Government is divided into fifteen ward offices, including the Kojimachi Ward Office, Kanda Ward Office, Nihonbashi Ward Office, Kyobashi Ward Office, Shiba Ward Office, Azabu Ward Office, Akasaka Ward Office, Yotsuya Ward Office, Ushigome Ward Office, Koishikawa Ward Office, Hongō Ward Office, Shitaya Ward Office, Asakusa Ward Office, Honjo Ward Office, and Fukagawa Ward Office. Each ward has a ward council with a total of 588 councilors, all serving in honorary positions. Each ward also has ten school affairs committee members, totaling 150, who are paid positions. Initially, the powers of the wards included both administrative and autonomous functions, handling the inherent affairs of the ward and the affairs entrusted by the city or the state. Since the implementation of the ward system on October 1, 1898, the wards have become fully autonomous local entities with independent finances. Each ward office is divided into five sections: general affairs, household registration, taxation, accounting, and hygiene and roads. Under the ward system, the village system is established based on the population and geographical conditions of each ward, similar to the villages in China. The area and population of each ward are listed below:

Kojimachi: Area 8,964,701 square meters, Population 60,600

Kanda: Area 3,864,366 square meters, Population 188,100

Nihonbashi: Area 2,867,719 square meters, Population 112,800

Kyobashi: Area 4,239,461 square meters, Population 119,300

Shiba: Area 9,030,383 square meters, Population 184,300

Azabu: Area 3,833,305 square meters, Population 100,400

Akasaka: Area 4,643,100 square meters, Population 65,600

Yotsuya: Area 1,289,586 square meters, Population 80,500

Ushigome: Area 5,035,824 square meters, Population 139,500

Koishikawa: Area 6,204,036 square meters, Population 163,900

Hongō: Area 5,099,758 square meters, Population 145,000

Shitaya: Area 4,830,743 square meters, Population 185,400

Asakusa: Area 4,832,211 square meters, Population 249,200

Honjo: Area 5,621,024 square meters, Population 222,500

Fukagawa: Area 7,845,091 square meters, Population 172,100

The total area of the fifteen wards is 79,960,655 square meters, and the total population is 2,143,200. Among them, Shiba Ward has the largest area, and Asakusa Ward has the largest population.

(Yin) A Brief Overview of the Tokyo City Council: Tokyo, with a population of nearly two million and an annual budget of approximately 300 million, is the center of Japanese politics, economy, and academia. In addition to the municipal office, which is the executive body, the deliberative body is the city council and the city council advisory body. City councilors are elected by citizens for a term of four years and serve in honorary positions. There are 84 councilors. Their functions include the enactment and amendment of city ordinances, the determination of the budget, the approval of the final accounts, the imposition and collection of city taxes, usage fees, and handling fees, and the determination of the management methods of city property and construction projects. The city council advisory body has twelve advisory members who are also elected for honorary positions. Their functions include initiating proposals for the expansion of city undertakings and submitting written opinions related to the administrative departments to the city council.

Reasons for the Particularly Large Settlements Yesterday 213

The foreign exchange market has been unusually tight for several days, and imports of goods have been halted. Foreign firms have nothing to do. Uncompleted transactions from the past have not been quickly settled, and there is no need for new transactions to be settled. The sudden influx of such a large amount of settlements yesterday has attracted the attention of the business community. After investigation, several reasons were found: (1) The rise in the shilling and the fall in the Japanese exchange yesterday created a large difference. Generally, those who had outstanding foreign exchange took the opportunity to close out their positions and offset their gold futures positions to balance their accounts. Therefore, the amount of settlements for this item yesterday was quite large. (2) A certain bank needed to settle over 4 million yuan yesterday for goods it had ordered from overseas. (3) There have been many instances of orders not being fulfilled recently, but some are still acknowledging losses. The result of yesterday's settlements was that the total amount of losses exceeded 1 million yuan. The above three types of settlements all had a significant release yesterday, so it is appropriate that the quantity was particularly large.

[P Grain>

More Than 400,000 Bags of Foreign Rice Arrive in Shanghai

Various Goods Down About 2 Jiao Yesterday

Yesterday, another ship carrying about 70-80,000 bags of foreign rice arrived, imported by Ding Muwan. Including the three ships that arrived the day before, there were a total of more than 400,000 bags, mostly shipped from Rangoon. After this batch arrived, merchants' intentions were weak, and they remained in a wait-and-see attitude, so the market suddenly fell by 2 jiao yesterday. However, the cargo owners had mostly pre-sold futures for this rice, and there was not much stock in the market, so they were not willing to depreciate the price greatly and unload lightly. However, people's confidence had been shaken. Overall, the city paper was 8-9,000 bags, and the price was about 2 jiao less, it is said.

Frenzied Flour Market 219

Spot Flour Has a Large Amount of Military Demand… Bulls Release Prices to Absorb

Standard Flour Exceeds Normal Limits… Each Month Rises Wildly by Six or Seven Cents

Yesterday, the flour market opened in the morning with a good situation, but the increase was still insignificant. By the time the afternoon session opened, many outside bears were frantically covering their positions, and it was heard that the government was purchasing spot flour due to military rations. In this state of frenzied excitement, this unexpected business gave the speculators even more support to raise prices, and new flour gradually rose. Large factories stood by and refused to sell off, leading the bulls to believe that since the factories were not selling, there was no need to worry. As a result, during the current month, prices were frequently released and purchased, as if the rise in prices would be as unlimited as the price of gold. As a result, the current month rose wildly by 7 fen compared to the previous day, July rose 6 fen 2.5 li, August rose 6 fen 5 li, September rose 6 fen, October rose 4 fen 5 li, and November rose 4 fen, it is said.

Soaring Prices of New Central Wheat 220

Buying Interest is Intense… Bears Compete to Cover

Yesterday, the market for wheat futures in each month showed a consistent and sharp rise. It is found that the driving force for this kind of surge actually started from the soaring price of gold. Because nervous people thought that without the small foreign flour wheat price, there would be no possibility of coming to China, although a small number of new wheat had already appeared on the market, the weather during the flood season was not seen to be very bad, and the Hubei gangs' thinking was even more firm and rising. The frenzy of buying interest and the smoothness of transactions in recent days are rare. Seeing this situation, because the big bears are thinking about making up for it, there are still signs of continued improvement. In the afternoon closing, as a result, June rose sharply by another 7 fen compared to the previous day, July rose 6 fen, August rose 7 fen, September rose 9 fen, October rose 5 fen, and November rose 6 fen. New and Old: The spot wheat market situation is that the standard has soared, and customers are gradually calling higher prices, raising them by another 3 fen compared to the previous day. Old wheat from Suzhou Qingjiangpu opened at 5 taels 0 fen 7 li, totaling 1,000 bags. Also, new wheat, such as Penglai Zhen wheat, was 4 taels 6 qian 5 fen, 4 taels 6 qian 3 fen, 4 taels 6 qian 4 fen, and 4 taels 5 qian 7 fen. Pudong wheat was 4 taels 4 qian 7 fen and 4 taels 3 qian 5 fen. Shuangfeng wheat was 4 taels 7 qian and 4 taels 6 qian 8 fen. Waigang wheat was 4 taels 5 qian 8 fen, totaling 3,000 bags, it is said.

Sugar Market 221

Jian Bing Tightens Due to Rising Raw Material Prices

Recently, Jian Bing has been extremely scarce in the market because the Dragon Boat Festival has passed, but the inventory of each company is still thick, so the market situation is even more difficult to rise. However, the spot price of raw sugar has been increasing step by step in recent days, and the trend is quite strong. Therefore, Jian Bing is also tightening accordingly. According to telegrams from various factories in Xiamen, the raw materials have risen and they are requesting to hold on. Therefore, the companies here are unanimously shouting for price increases. Dealers have some stock on hand and are temporarily unwilling to add immediately, and are holding back.

Silk and Tea 222

Chaotic Exchange Rates Make the Silk Market Even Quieter

Yesterday, the silk market in Shanghai continued to trend towards calm. Since the surge in gold prices, exchange rates have repeatedly changed, and the export industry has been greatly affected. American and Japanese firms originally intended to expand new factories, but the exchange rate shrank by several levels every day, making it difficult to proceed. The attitude of the manufacturers remained firm, and the market was suspended again yesterday.

Tea Market Becomes Increasingly Desolate 223

Yesterday, there were no large transactions for black tea from Qimen and Ningzhou. No one asked about Road Estate and Native Estate Fancy Eyebrow tea. Only Pingshui Pearl Tea from Tongfu Yih and other firms had some interest. The market situation was unusually quiet. It is found that the reason for the recent market downturn is actually due to the soaring price of gold, chaotic exchange rates, and people's minds are floating, and everyone is holding a wait-and-see attitude, it is said.

Qifu Zicha (Second Flush Tea) Has Already Shown Buds 224

Qifu Xiazhuang Zicha, due to the suitable sunny and rainy weather in the past month, the tea trees in Zhouyuan have already shown buds. According to the mountain households, this year's Zicha is more vigorous than the first flush tea, and the quality and taste are also better. The output will definitely be abundant in the future. Due to the high and profitable sales of the first batch of tea, Qifu's various firms are paying special attention to Zicha because the number of boxes this year has been sharply reduced. Many tea firms are planning to finish the three-character production and prepare to continue running Xiazhuang.

Coal 225

Coal Market Amidst Soaring Marking Gold

Chaotic Market… Various Goods Rise by One or Two Taels

In recent days, marking gold has soared, and the foreign exchange rate has frequently shrunk. The market price of coal in Shanghai is very chaotic, sometimes high and sometimes low, making it difficult to grasp. In the most recent three days, the goods sold have no fixed price, and those who need to buy from the Lilu gang are temporarily unable to start. Qingfeng Garden

Xin You Troupe Performing Today 231

The Xin You Troupe is putting on a difficult play series this time to improve theatrical art. The first play (Uncle Wen) was performed last week and won a lot of praise from the theatrical and literary circles. The second play (Dancing Under the Dog) will be staged today (the 7th) at the Central Auditorium on North Sichuan Road.

Introduction to the Famous Play (Dancing Under the Dog) by Zhang Er 232

Since the Xin You Troupe performed Andrive's (Dancing Under the Dog) last year, it has created amazing achievements and broken all previous records in the theatrical art world. Even now, it is still in the minds of artists and dramatists with a very deep impression. Now they are working hard again to do a difficult play movement. (Dancing Under the Dog) is actually re-staging in this movement on the seventh of this month (today). Taking this opportunity, I will write down my impressions from last year and make a solemn introduction to art lovers.

First, let's talk about the story of the script. Zhai Hanli is a shrewd and capable employee of a certain bank. His fiancée, Mo Licai, is a smart and beautiful woman. They have set a date for their wedding, and Hanli is excitedly preparing for the wedding and arranging the future home. Suddenly, a thunderbolt struck out of the blue. His fiancée was plundered by someone using economic means. Struck by this blow, he became decadent and evil. On one hand, he harbored hatred for the rich, and he wanted to steal a large sum of money from the bank to avenge himself. What about Licai? She did not want to remarry someone else. What's more, not long after the marriage, her husband and her children both died. So she ran to find Hanli. Hanli, who had a very strong personality and was unwilling to forgive, drove her out. She was extremely sad and her psychology changed. She also fell. She had money, and she could find some men to vent her sexual desires, but what she kept thinking about was still wanting to go to Hanli's house to linger for a while, to pay tribute, and to cry bitterly. The result was that Hanli's first goal was achieved. He stole the money from the bank, but the psychological changes over the years made him feel empty and unable to fill it. In addition, because of his immersion in wine and sex, he became haggard and old. He felt that he was unable to do anything, so he decided to commit suicide.

The source of the play title (Dancing Under the Dog) is because the protagonist Zhai Hanli is a very lonely person who does not have the leisure and elegance. The reason why his home has musical equipment is because his fiancée is skilled in music. He himself does not know much about music, but when he was a child, his mother taught him a simple tune called (Dancing Under the Dog). Even when he grew up, he has not forgotten it. When he was happy, he played it for his lover and his friends to listen to. Although his fingering was very clumsy, when he became decadent, he played it for his patrons to listen to. When he was sad, desperate and committed suicide, he played it for himself to listen to. It was played four or five times in the play, so the author symbolized the whole play's melancholy and depression with that tune.

Andrive's philosophy is gray and full of mystery. Of course, (Dancing Under the Dog) is also like that, so many people in last year's audience did not understand the play's purpose even after watching the whole play. My personal interpretation is that the play symbolizes the depressing emotions of the chaotic era before the Russian War. The protagonist's disappointment, struggle, and despair is the whole process of the play. Isn't Zhai Hanli's catchphrase (The door will close by itself) clearly referring to (People always have to die) or (Everything ends up being empty)? He also said, (I used to live, live) and (All kinds of pasts are there, all kinds of pasts are empty). This is exactly Andrive's desperate philosophy. The script also says, "Who is it that has not been born? Who is it that has not seen the light?" How he misses his descendants and longs for the indefinite future light of mankind! (The sun will rise at seven o'clock, how can I spend this flowery black night?) Zhai Hanli could not wait for the light of tomorrow, just as Andrive could not wait for the future light. What a sad writer! The play was performed by the Xin You Troupe, and the director is also the translator. Of course, the meaning of the script is fully expressed. Their performance art is second to none on the Shanghai theater stage. What I like most is that they create very grand sets. Although there are a few large props on the stage, it still feels very desolate. When Zhai Hanli's heart is fighting between the two thoughts of life and death and he is dancing madly on the stage, you can see that this person is as small as an insect and as dim as a ghost, creating a kind of tragic air that makes the audience feel that he really can't live. In addition, Mr. Yuan Muzhi's performance in the role of Zhai Hanli is exquisite, fully portraying Zhai Hanli's profound inner world, and implying the entire history of Zhai Hanli, which can be written with five or six hundred thousand words, in the four-act play. This is very commendable.

In a theater world that is keen on low-level tastes, the Xin You Troupe's difficult drama movement is indeed rare and valuable.

Zhai Hanli in the third act of Dancing the Dog (played by Yuan Muzhi)
